The Crown Plaza Hotel was an absolute delight. From the moment I stepped through the grand, ornate entryway, I was struck by the elegant, timeless decor and impeccable service. My room was spacious and luxurious, with plush bedding, a marble bathroom, and breathtaking views of the city skyline. The hotel's central location also made it easy to explore the surrounding neighborhood's charming shops and landmarks.

posted:Posted May 5, 2024
msg:The hotel is located outside the Third Ring Road. It seems to be very remote, but it is actually very suitable for self-driving tours. Because it is only half an hour's drive to the main scenic spots in Wuhan, and even during the May Day holiday, there is no traffic jam (if you live in the city center, a little traffic jam will actually pass half an hour). Next to it is Wanda Plaza, and there are very rich choices for eating and shopping. There are not so many people eating during the May Day holiday, and there is no need to queue even for Internet celebrity restaurants. The hotel has ample parking lots, and there are many high-power charging piles next to the hotel. Parking and charging are super convenient.
The executive room we booked includes the executive lounge, and the children like to eat in it. The breakfast is quite rich, and you can choose to have breakfast on the lawn outside, which feels very fresh.
Opposite should be the headquarters of Dongfeng Motor. There are many driverless cars being tested on the road, and you can take your children to see it.
